He will die for lack of discipline, and in the greatness of his folly he will go astray.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 6
בְּנִי אִם־עָרַבְתָּ לְרֵעֶךָ תָּקַעְתָּ לַזָּר כַּפֶּיךָ׃
נוֹקַשְׁתָּ בְאִמְרֵי פִיךָ נִלְכַּדְתָּ בְאִמְרֵי פִיךָ׃
עֲשֵׂה־זֹּאת אֵפוֹא בְּנִי וְהִנָּצֵל כִּי בָאתָ בְכַף־רֵעֶךָ לֵךְ הִתְרַפֵּס וּרְהַב רֵעֶיךָ׃
אַל־תִּתֵּן שֵׁנָה לְעֵינֶיךָ וּתְנוּמָה לְעַפְעַפֶּיךָ׃
הִנָּצֵל כִּצְבִי מִיָּד וּכְצִפּוֹר מִיַּד יָקוּשׁ׃
לֵךְ אֶל־נְמָלָה עָצֵל רְאֵה דְרָכֶיהָ וַחֲכָם׃
אֲשֶׁר אֵין־לָהּ קָצִין שֹׁטֵר וּמֹשֵׁל׃
תָּכִין בַּקַּיִץ לַחְמָהּ אָגְרָה בַקָּצִיר מַאֲכָלָהּ׃
עַד־מָתַי עָצֵל תִּשְׁכָּב מָתַי תָּקוּם מִשְּׁנָתֶךָ׃
מְעַט שֵׁנוֹת מְעַט תְּנוּמוֹת מְעַט חִבֻּק יָדַיִם לִשְׁכָּב׃
וּבָא כִמְהַלֵּךְ רֵישֶׁךָ וּמַחְסֹרֶךָ כְּאִישׁ מָגֵן׃
אָדָם בְּלִיַּעַל אִישׁ אָוֶן הוֹלֵךְ עִקְּשׁוּת פֶּה׃
קֹרֵץ בְּעֵינָיו מֹלֵל בְּרַגְלָיו מוֹרֶה בְּאֶצְבְּעֹתָיו׃
תַּהְפֻּכוֹת בְּלִבּוֹ חֹרֵשׁ רָע בְּכָל־עֵת מְדָנִים יְשַׁלֵּחַ׃
עַל־כֵּן פִּתְאֹם יָבוֹא אֵידוֹ פֶּתַע יִשָּׁבֵר וְאֵין מַרְפֵּא׃
שֵׁשׁ הֵנָּה שָׂנֵא יְהוָה וְשֶׁבַע תּוֹעֲבוֹת נַפְשׁוֹ׃
עֵינַיִם רָמוֹת לְשׁוֹן שָׁקֶר וְיָדַיִם שֹׁפְכוֹת דָּם נָקִי׃
לֵב חֹרֵשׁ מַחְשְׁבוֹת אָוֶן רַגְלַיִם מְמַהֲרוֹת לָרוּץ לָרָעָה׃
יָפִיחַ כְּזָבִים עֵד שָׁקֶר וּמְשַׁלֵּחַ מְדָנִים בֵּין אַחִים׃
נְצֹר בְּנִי מִצְוַת אָבִיךָ וְאַל־תִּטֹּשׁ תּוֹרַת אִמֶּךָ׃
קָשְׁרֵם עַל־לִבֶּךָ תָמִיד עָנְדֵם עַל־גַּרְגְּרֹתֶיךָ׃
בְּהִתְהַלֶּכְךָ תַּנְחֶה אֹתָךְ בְּשָׁכְבְּךָ תִּשְׁמֹר עָלֶיךָ וַהֲקִיצוֹתָ הִיא תְשִׂיחֶךָ׃
כִּי נֵר מִצְוָה וְתוֹרָה אוֹר וְדֶרֶךְ חַיִּים תּוֹכְחוֹת מוּסָר׃
לִשְׁמָרְךָ מֵאֵשֶׁת רָע מֵחֶלְקַת לָשׁוֹן נָכְרִיָּה׃
אַל־תַּחְמֹד יָפְיָהּ בִּלְבָבֶךָ וְאַל־תִּקָּחֲךָ בְּעַפְעַפֶּיהָ׃
כִּי בְעַד־אִשָּׁה זוֹנָה עַד־כִּכַּר־לָחֶם וְאֵשֶׁת אִישׁ נֶפֶשׁ יְקָרָה תָצוּד׃
הֲיַחְתֶּה אִישׁ אֵשׁ בְּחֵיקוֹ וּבְגָדָיו לֹא תִשָּׂרַפְנָה׃
אִם־יְהַלֵּךְ אִישׁ עַל־הַגֶּחָלִים וְרַגְלָיו לֹא תִכָּוֶינָה׃
כֵּן הַבָּא אֶל־אֵשֶׁת רֵעֵהוּ לֹא יִנָּקֶה כָּל־הַנֹּגֵעַ בָּהּ׃
לֹא־יָבוּזוּ לַגַּנָּב כִּי יִגְנוֹב לְמַלֵּא נַפְשׁוֹ כִּי יִרְעָב׃
וְנִמְצָא יְשַׁלֵּם שִׁבְעָתָיִם אֶת־כָּל־הוֹן בֵּיתוֹ יִתֵּן׃
נֹאֵף אִשָּׁה חֲסַר־לֵב מַשְׁחִית נַפְשׁוֹ הוּא יַעֲשֶׂנָּה׃
נֶגַע וְקָלוֹן יִמְצָא וְחֶרְפָּתוֹ לֹא תִמָּחֶה׃
כִּי־קִנְאָה חֲמַת־גָּבֶר וְלֹא־יַחְמוֹל בְּיוֹם נָקָם׃
לֹא־יִשָּׂא פְנֵי כָל־כֹּפֶר וְלֹא יֹאבֶה כִּי־תַרְבֶּה שֹׁחַד׃
My son, if you have become surety for your neighbor, if you have struck your hands for a stranger,
you are snared by the words of your mouth; you are caught by the words of your mouth.
Do this then, my son, and deliver yourself, since you have come into the hand of your neighbor: go, humble yourself and press your neighbor.
Give no sleep to your eyes nor slumber to your eyelids;
deliver yourself like a gazelle from the hand, and like a bird from the hand of the fowler.
Go to the ant, O sluggard; consider her ways and be wise,
which, having no chief, officer, or ruler,
prepares her bread in summer, gathers her food in harvest.
How long will you lie down, O sluggard? When will you arise from your sleep?
A little sleep, a little slumber, a little folding of the hands to lie down,
and your poverty will come like a traveler and your lack like an armed man.
A worthless person, a man of wickedness, walks with a perverse mouth,
winking with his eyes, speaking with his feet, pointing with his fingers,
perversity is in his heart, he devises evil continually, he sends out strife.
Therefore suddenly his calamity will come; suddenly he will be broken without remedy.
Six things YHWH hates, and seven are an abomination to his soul:
haughty eyes, a lying tongue, and hands that shed innocent blood,
a heart that devises wicked plans, feet that hurry to run to evil,
a false witness who breathes lies, and one who sends out strife among brothers.
Keep, my son, your father’s commandment, and do not forsake your mother’s teaching.
Bind them continually on your heart; tie them around your neck.
When you walk, they will guide you; when you lie down, they will watch over you; and when you awake, they will talk with you.
For the commandment is a lamp and the teaching is light, and reproofs of discipline are the way of life,
to guard you from the evil woman, from the smooth tongue of the foreign woman.
Do not desire her beauty in your heart, nor let her capture you with her eyelids,
for on account of a harlot one is reduced to a loaf of bread, but a married woman hunts a precious life.
Can a man carry fire in his bosom and his clothes not be burned?
Or can one walk on hot coals and his feet not be scorched?
So is he who goes in to his neighbor’s wife; none who touches her will go unpunished.
People do not despise a thief if he steals to satisfy his soul when he is hungry,
yet when he is found, he must repay sevenfold; he must give all the substance of his house.
He who commits adultery with a woman lacks heart; he who does it destroys his own soul.
Wound and dishonor he will find, and his reproach will not be wiped away,
for jealousy is the rage of a man, and he will not spare in the day of vengeance.
He will accept no ransom, nor will he be satisfied though you give many gifts.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 7
בְּנִי שְׁמֹר אֲמָרָי וּמִצְוֹתַי תִּצְפֹּן אִתָּךְ׃
שְׁמֹר מִצְוֹתַי וֶחְיֵה וְתוֹרָתִי כְּאִישׁוֹן עֵינֶיךָ׃
קָשְׁרֵם עַל־אֶצְבְּעֹתֶיךָ כָּתְבֵם עַל־לוּחַ לִבֶּךָ׃
אֱמֹר לַחָכְמָה אֲחֹתִי אָתְּ וּמֹדָע לַבִּינָה תִקְרָא׃
לִשְׁמָרְךָ מֵאִשָּׁה זָרָה מִנָּכְרִיָּה אֲמָרֶיהָ הֶחֱלִיקָה׃
כִּי בְּחַלּוֹן בֵּיתִי בְּעַד אֶשְׁנָבִי נִשְׁקָפְתִּי׃
וָאֵרֶא בַפְּתָאיִם אָבִינָה בַבָּנִים נַעַר חֲסַר־לֵב׃
עֹבֵר בַּשּׁוּק אֵצֶל פִּנָּהּ וְדֶרֶךְ בֵּיתָהּ יִצְעָד׃
בְּנֶשֶׁף בְּעֶרֶב יוֹם בְּאִישׁוֹן לַיְלָה וַאֲפֵלָה׃
וְהִנֵּה אִשָּׁה לִקְרָאתוֹ שִׁית זוֹנָה וּנְצֻרַת לֵב׃
הֹמִיָּה הִיא וְסֹרָרֶת בְּבֵיתָהּ לֹא יִשְׁכְּנוּ רַגְלֶיהָ׃
פַּעַם בַּחוּץ פַּעַם בָּרְחֹבוֹת וְאֵצֶל כָּל־פִּנָּה תֶאֱרֹב׃
וְהֶחֱזִיקָה בוֹ וְנָשְׁקָה לוֹ הֵעֵזָה פָנֶיהָ וַתֹּאמֶר לוֹ׃
זִבְחֵי שְׁלָמִים עָלָי הַיּוֹם שִׁלַּמְתִּי נְדָרָי׃
עַל־כֵּן יָצָאתִי לִקְרָאתֶךָ לְשַׁחֵר פָּנֶיךָ וָאֶמְצָאֶךָ׃
מַרְבַדִּים רָבַדְתִּי עַרְשִׂי חֲטֻבוֹת אֵטוּן מִצְרָיִם׃
נָפַתִּי מִשְׁכָּבִי מֹר אֲהָלִים וְקִנָּמוֹן׃
לְכָה נִרְוֶה דֹדִים עַד־הַבֹּקֶר נִתְעַלְּסָה בָּאֳהָבִים׃
כִּי אֵין הָאִישׁ בְּבֵיתוֹ הָלַךְ בְּדֶרֶךְ מֵרָחוֹק׃
צְרוֹר־הַכֶּסֶף לָקַח בְּיָדוֹ לְיוֹם הַכֵּסֶא יָבוֹא בֵיתוֹ׃
הִטַּתּוּ בְּרֹב לִקְחָהּ בְּחֶלְקַת שְׂפָתֶיהָ תַּדִּיחֶנּוּ׃
הוֹלֵךְ אַחֲרֶיהָ פִּתְאֹם כְּשׁוֹר אֶל־טֶבַח יָבוֹא וּכְעֶכֶס אֶל־מוּסַר אֱוִיל׃
עַד יְפַלַּח חֵץ כְּבֵדוֹ כְּמַהֵר צִפּוֹר אֶל־פָּח וְלֹא־יָדַע כִּי בְנַפְשׁוֹ הוּא׃
וְעַתָּה בָנִים שִׁמְעוּ־לִי וְהַקְשִׁיבוּ לְאִמְרֵי פִי׃
אַל־יֵשְׂטְ אֶל־דְּרָכֶיהָ לִבֶּךָ אַל־תֵּתַע בִּנְתִיבוֹתֶיהָ׃
כִּי־רַבִּים חֲלָלִים הִפִּילָה וַעֲצֻמִים כָּל־הֲרֻגֶיהָ׃
דַּרְכֵי שְׁאוֹל בֵּיתָהּ יֹרְדוֹת אֶל־חַדְרֵי־מָוֶת׃
My son, keep my words and treasure up my commandments with you.
Keep my commandments and live, and my teaching as the pupil of your eye.
Bind them on your fingers; write them on the tablet of your heart.
Say to wisdom, “You are my sister,” and call understanding a close friend,
to keep you from the strange woman, from the foreign woman who smooths her words.
For at the window of my house, through my lattice I looked out,
and I saw among the simple, I discerned among the youths, a young man lacking heart,
passing along the street near her corner, taking the way to her house,
in the twilight, in the evening of the day, in the blackness of night and darkness.
And behold, a woman comes to meet him, dressed like a prostitute and guarded of heart.
She is loud and rebellious; her feet do not stay at home.
Now in the street, now in the squares, and at every corner she lies in wait.
And she seizes him and kisses him; with a bold face she says to him:
“I had peace offerings upon me; today I have paid my vows.
So now I have come out to meet you, to seek your face, and I have found you.
I have spread my couch with coverings, colored linens of Egypt.
I have perfumed my bed with myrrh, aloes, and cinnamon.
Come, let us drink deeply of love until morning; let us delight ourselves with loves.
For the man is not at home; he has gone on a long journey.
He took a bag of money with him; at the full moon he will come home.”
She persuades him with much persuasion; with the smoothness of her lips she compels him.
Suddenly he goes after her, like an ox going to the slaughter, or like a fetter to the discipline of a fool,
until an arrow pierces his liver; as a bird hastens to the snare, and does not know that it is for his life.
And now, sons, listen to me, and pay attention to the words of my mouth.
Do not let your heart turn aside to her ways; do not stray into her paths.
For many are the slain she has cast down, and numerous are all her killed.
Her house is the way to Sheol, going down to the chambers of death.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 8
הֲלֹא חָכְמָה תִקְרָא וּתְבוּנָה תִּתֵּן קוֹלָהּ׃
בְּרֹאשׁ מְרוֹמִים עֲלֵי דָרֶךְ בֵּית נְתִיבוֹת נִצָּבָה׃
עַל־יַד שְׁעָרִים לְפִי־קָרֶת מְבוֹא פְתָחִים תָּרֹנָּה׃
אֲלֵיכֶם אִישִׁים אֶקְרָא וְקוֹלִי אֶל־בְּנֵי אָדָם׃
הָבִינוּ פְתָאיִם עָרְמָה וּכְסִילִים הָבִינוּ לֵב׃
שִׁמְעוּ כִּי־נְגִידִים אֲדַבֵּר וּמִפְתַּח שְׂפָתַי מֵישָׁרִים׃
כִּי־אֱמֶת יֶהְגֶּה חִכִּי וְתוֹעֲבַת שְׂפָתַי רֶשַׁע׃
בְּצֶדֶק כָּל־אִמְרֵי פִי אֵין בָּהֶם נִפְתָּל וְעִקֵּשׁ׃
כֻּלָּם נְכֹחִים לְמֵבִין וִישָׁרִים לְמֹצְאֵי דָעַת׃
קְחוּ מוּסָרִי וְאַל־כָּסֶף וְדַעַת מֵחָרוּץ נִבְחָר׃
כִּי־טוֹבָה חָכְמָה מִפְּנִינִים וְכָל־חֲפָצִים לֹא יִשְׁווּ בָהּ׃
אֲנִי חָכְמָה שָׁכַנְתִּי עָרְמָה וְדַעַת מְזִמּוֹת אֶמְצָא׃
יִרְאַת יְהוָה שְׂנֹאת רָע גֵּאָה וְגָאוֹן וְדֶרֶךְ רָע וּפִי תַהְפֻּכוֹת שָׂנֵאתִי׃
לִי עֵצָה וְתוּשִׁיָּה אֲנִי בִינָה לִי גְבוּרָה׃
בִּי מְלָכִים יִמְלֹכוּ וְרוֹזְנִים יְחֹקְקוּ צֶדֶק׃
בִּי שָׂרִים יָשֹׂרוּ וּנְדִיבִים כָּל־שֹׁפְטֵי צֶדֶק׃
אֲנִי אֹהֲבַי אָהֵב וּמְשַׁחֲרַי יִמְצָאֻנְנִי׃
עֹשֶׁר וְכָבוֹד אִתִּי הוֹן עָתֵק וּצְדָקָה׃
טוֹב פִּרְיִי מֵחָרוּץ וּמִפָּז וּתְבוּאָתִי מִכֶּסֶף נִבְחָר׃
בְּאֹרַח צְדָקָה אֲהַלֵּךְ בְּתוֹךְ נְתִיבוֹת מִשְׁפָּט׃
לְהַנְחִיל אֹהֲבַי יֵשׁ וְאֹצְרוֹתֵיהֶם אֲמַלֵּא׃
יְהוָה קָנָנִי רֵאשִׁית דַּרְכּוֹ קֶדֶם מִפְעָלָיו מֵאָז׃
מֵעוֹלָם נִסַּכְתִּי מֵרֹאשׁ מִקַּדְמֵי־אָרֶץ׃
בְּאֵין תְּהֹמוֹת חוֹלָלְתִּי בְּאֵין מַעְיָנוֹת נִכְבָּדֵי־מָיִם׃
בְּטֶרֶם הָרִים הָטְבָּעוּ לִפְנֵי גְּבָעוֹת חוֹלָלְתִּי׃
עַד־לֹא עָשָׂה אֶרֶץ וְחוּצוֹת וְרֹאשׁ עַפְרוֹת תֵּבֵל׃
בַּהֲכִינוֹ שָׁמַיִם שָׁם אָנִי בְּחוּקוֹ חוּג עַל־פְּנֵי תְהוֹם׃
בְּאַמְצוֹ שְׁחָקִים מִמָּעַל בַּעֲזוֹז עִינוֹת תְּהוֹם׃
בְּשׂוּמוֹ לַיָּם חֻקּוֹ וּמַיִם לֹא יַעַבְרוּ פִיו בְּחוּקוֹ מוֹסְדֵי אָרֶץ׃
וָאֶהְיֶה אֶצְלוֹ אָמוֹן וָאֶהְיֶה שַׁעֲשֻׁעִים יוֹם יוֹם מְשַׂחֶקֶת לְפָנָיו בְּכָל־עֵת׃
מְשַׂחֶקֶת בְּתֵבֵל אַרְצוֹ וְשַׁעֲשֻׁעַי אֶת־בְּנֵי אָדָם׃
וְעַתָּה בָנִים שִׁמְעוּ־לִי וְאַשְׁרֵי דַרְכֵי יִשְׁמֹרוּ׃
שִׁמְעוּ מוּסָר וַחֲכָמוּ וְאַל־תִּפְרָעוּ׃
אַשְׁרֵי אָדָם שֹׁמֵעַ לִי לִשְׁקֹד עַל־דַּלְתֹתַי יוֹם יוֹם לִשְׁמֹר מְזוּזוֹת פְּתָחָי׃
כִּי מֹצְאִי מָצָא חַיִּים וַיִּפֶק רָצוֹן מֵיְהוָה׃
וְחֹטְאִי חֹמֵס נַפְשׁוֹ כָּל־מְשַׂנְאַי אָהֲבוּ מָוֶת׃
Does not Wisdom call, and Understanding lift up her voice?
On the heights beside the way, at the crossroads she takes her stand;
beside the gates, at the entrance of the city, at the entry doors she cries out:
“To you, O men, I call, and my voice is to the sons of man.
Understand, simple ones, prudence; and fools, understand heart.
Listen, for I speak noble things, and the opening of my lips is right.
For my mouth will utter truth, and wickedness is an abomination to my lips.
All the words of my mouth are in righteousness; nothing twisted or crooked in them.
They are all straight to him who understands and right to those who find knowledge.
Take my instruction and not silver, and knowledge rather than choice gold.
For wisdom is better than jewels, and all desirable things cannot compare with her.
I, Wisdom, dwell with prudence, and I find knowledge and discretion.
The fear of YHWH is hatred of evil; pride, arrogance, the way of evil, and perverse speech I hate.
Counsel and sound wisdom are mine; I am understanding; I have strength.
By me kings reign, and rulers decree justice.
By me princes rule, and nobles—all who govern justly.
I love those who love me, and those who seek me diligently find me.
Riches and honor are with me, enduring wealth and righteousness.
My fruit is better than gold, even fine gold, and my yield than choice silver.
I walk in the way of righteousness, in the paths of justice,
to endow those who love me with wealth and fill their treasuries.
YHWH possessed me at the beginning of his way, before his works of old.
From eternity I was set up, from the beginning, before the earth was.
When there were no depths I was brought forth, when there were no springs abounding with water.
Before the mountains were settled, before the hills I was brought forth,
before he made the earth and fields and the first dust of the world.
When he established the heavens, I was there; when he drew a circle on the face of the deep,
when he made firm the skies above, when he strengthened the fountains of the deep,
when he assigned to the sea its limit, so that the waters would not transgress his command,
when he marked out the foundations of the earth,
then I was beside him, like a master craftsman, and I was daily his delight, rejoicing before him always,
rejoicing in his inhabited world and delighting in the sons of man.
And now, sons, listen to me; blessed are those who keep my ways.
Hear instruction and be wise, and do not neglect it.
Blessed is the man who listens to me, watching daily at my doors,
for whoever finds me finds life and obtains favor from YHWH,
but he who sins against me injures his own soul; all who hate me love death.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 9
חָכְמוֹת בָּנְתָה בֵיתָהּ חָצְבָה עַמּוּדֶיהָ שִׁבְעָה׃
טָבְחָה טִבְחָהּ מָסְכָה יֵינָהּ אַף עָרְכָה שֻׁלְחָנָהּ׃
שָׁלְחָה נַעֲרֹתֶיהָ תִּקְרָא עַל־גַּפֵּי מְרֹמֵי קָרֶת׃
מִי פֶתִי יָסֻר הֵנָּה חֲסַר־לֵב אָמְרָה לוֹ׃
לְכוּ לַחֲמוּ בְלַחֲמִי וּשְׁתוּ בְּיַיִן מָסָכְתִּי׃
עִזְבוּ פְתָאיִם וִחְיוּ וְאִשְׁרוּ בְּדֶרֶךְ בִּינָה׃
יֹסֵר לֵץ לֹקֵחַ לוֹ קָלוֹן וּמוֹכִיחַ לְרָשָׁע מוּמוֹ׃
אַל־תּוֹכַח לֵץ פֶּן־יִשְׂנָאֶךָּ הוֹכַח לְחָכָם וְיֶאֱהָבֶךָּ׃
תֵּן לְחָכָם וְיֶחְכַּם עוֹד הוֹדַע לְצַדִּיק וְיוֹסֶף לֶקַח׃
תְּחִלַּת חָכְמָה יִרְאַת יְהוָה וְדַעַת קְדֹשִׁים בִּינָה׃
כִּי־בִי יִרְבּוּ יָמֶיךָ וְיוֹסִיפוּ לְךָ שְׁנוֹת חַיִּים׃
אִם־חָכַמְתָּ חָכַמְתָּ לָּךְ וְלַצַּתְּ לְבַדְּךָ תִשָּׂא׃
אֵשֶׁת כְּסִילוּת הֹמִיָּה פְּתַיּוּת וּבַל־יָדְעָה מָה׃
וְיָשְׁבָה לְפֶתַח בֵּיתָהּ עַל־כִּסֵּא מְרֹמֵי קָרֶת׃
לִקְרֹא לְעֹבְרֵי דָרֶךְ הַמְיַשְּׁרִים אֹרְחוֹתָם׃
מִי־פֶתִי יָסֻר הֵנָּה וַחֲסַר־לֵב וְאָמְרָה לוֹ׃
מַיִם גְּנוּבִים יִמְתָּקוּ וְלֶחֶם סְתָרִים יִנְעָם׃
וְלֹא יָדַע כִּי־רְפָאִים שָׁם בְּעִמְקֵי שְׁאוֹל קְרֻאֶיהָ׃
Wisdom has built her house; she has hewn her seven pillars.
She has slaughtered her meat, mixed her wine, and also set her table.
She has sent out her young women; she calls from the highest places of the city:
“Whoever is simple, let him turn in here!” To one lacking heart she says:
“Come, eat of my bread, and drink of the wine I have mixed.
Leave the simple ones and live, and walk in the way of understanding.”
Whoever corrects a scoffer gets dishonor for himself, and whoever rebukes the wicked gets insult.
Do not reprove a scoffer, lest he hate you; reprove a wise man, and he will love you.
Give instruction to a wise man, and he will become still wiser; teach a righteous man, and he will increase in learning.
The fear of YHWH is the beginning of wisdom, and knowledge of the Holy One is understanding.
For by me your days will be multiplied, and years of life will be added to you.
If you are wise, you are wise for yourself; and if you scoff, you alone will bear it.
The woman of folly is loud; she is simple and knows nothing.
She sits at the door of her house, on a seat in the high places of the city,
calling to those who pass by, who go straight on their ways:
“Whoever is simple, let him turn in here!” And to one lacking heart she says:
“Stolen waters are sweet, and bread eaten in secret is pleasant.”
But he does not know that the dead are there, that her guests are in the depths of Sheol.


======Proverbs 10–22:16

>>>>>>> Proverbs 10
מִשְׁלֵי שְׁלֹמֹה בֵּן־חָכָם יְשַׂמַּח אָב וּבֵן כְּסִיל תּוּגַת אִמּוֹ׃
לֹא־יוֹעִילוּ אוֹצְרוֹת רֶשַׁע וּצְדָקָה תַּצִּיל מִמָּוֶת׃
לֹא־יַרְעִיב יְהוָה נֶפֶשׁ צַדִּיק וְהַוַּת רְשָׁעִים יֶהְדֹּף׃
רָאשׁ עֹשֶׂה כַף־רְמִיָּה וְיַד חָרוּצִים תַּעֲשִׁיר׃
אֹגֵר בַּקַּיִץ בֵּן מַשְׂכִּיל נִרְדָּם בַּקָּצִיר בֵּן מֵבִישׁ׃
בְּרָכוֹת לְרֹאשׁ צַדִּיק וּפִי רְשָׁעִים יְכַסֶּה חָמָס׃
זֵכֶר צַדִּיק לִבְרָכָה וְשֵׁם רְשָׁעִים יִרְקָב׃
חֲכַם לֵב יִקַּח מִצְוֹת וֶאֱוִיל שְׂפָתַיִם יִלָּבֵט׃
הוֹלֵךְ בַּתֹּם יֵלֶךְ בֶּטַח וּמְעַקֵּשׁ דְּרָכָיו יִוָּדֵעַ׃
קֹרֵץ עַיִן יִתֵּן עַצֶּבֶת וֶאֱוִיל שְׂפָתַיִם יִלָּבֵט׃
מְקוֹר חַיִּים פִּי צַדִּיק וּפִי רְשָׁעִים יְכַסֶּה חָמָס׃
שִׂנְאָה תְּעוֹרֵר מְדָנִים וְעַל כָּל־פְּשָׁעִים תְּכַסֶּה אַהֲבָה׃
בְּשִׂפְתֵי נָבוֹן תִּמָּצֵא חָכְמָה וְשֵׁבֶט לְגֵו חֲסַר־לֵב׃
חֲכָמִים יִצְפְּנוּ דָעַת וּפִי אֱוִיל מְחִתָּה קְרוֹבָה׃
הוֹן עָשִׁיר קִרְיַת עֻזּוֹ מְחִתַּת דַּלִּים רֵישָׁם׃
פְּעֻלַּת צַדִּיק לְחַיִּים תְּבוּאַת רָשָׁע לְחַטָּאת׃
אוֹרַח לְחַיִּים שׁוֹמֵר מוּסָר וְעֹזֵב תּוֹכַחַת מַתְעֶה׃
מְכַסֶּה שִׂנְאָה שִׂפְתֵי שָׁקֶר וּמוֹצִא דִבָּה הוּא כְסִיל׃
בְּרֹב דְּבָרִים לֹא יֶחְדַּל פָּשַׁע וְחֹשֵׂךְ שְׂפָתָיו מַשְׂכִּיל׃
כֶּסֶף נִבְחָר לְשׁוֹן צַדִּיק לֵב רְשָׁעִים כִּמְעָט׃
שִׂפְתֵי צַדִּיק יִרְעוּ רַבִּים וֶאֱוִילִים בַּחֲסַר־לֵב יָמוּתוּ׃
בִּרְכַּת יְהוָה הִיא תַעֲשִׁיר וְלֹא יוֹסִיף עֶצֶב עִמָּהּ׃
כְּשְׂחוֹק לִכְסִיל עֲשׂוֹת זִמָּה וְחָכְמָה לְאִישׁ תְּבוּנָה׃
מְגוֹרַת רָשָׁע הִיא תָבוֹאֶנּוּ וְתַאֲוַת צַדִּיקִים יִתֵּן׃
כַּעֲבוֹר סוּפָה וְאֵין רָשָׁע וְצַדִּיק יְסוֹד עוֹלָם׃
כְּחֹמֶץ לַשִּׁנַּיִם וְכְעָשָׁן לָעֵינָיִם כֵּן הֶעָצֵל לְשֹׁלְחָיו׃
יִרְאַת יְהוָה תּוֹסִיף יָמִים וּשְׁנוֹת רְשָׁעִים תִּקְצֹרְנָה׃
תּוֹחֶלֶת צַדִּיקִים שִׂמְחָה וְתִקְוַת רְשָׁעִים תֹּאבֵד׃
מָעוֹז לַתֹּם דֶּרֶךְ יְהוָה וּמְחִתָּה לְפֹעֲלֵי אָוֶן׃
צַדִּיק לְעוֹלָם בַּל־יִמּוֹט וּרְשָׁעִים לֹא יִשְׁכְּנוּ־אָרֶץ׃
פִּי צַדִּיק יַנְבִּיעַ חָכְמָה וּלְשׁוֹן תַּהְפֻּכוֹת תִּכָּרֵת׃
שִׂפְתֵי צַדִּיק יֵדְעוּן רָצוֹן וּפִי רְשָׁעִים תַּהְפֻּכוֹת׃
The proverbs of Solomon. A wise son makes a father glad, but a foolish son is his mother’s sorrow.
Treasures of wickedness do not profit, but righteousness delivers from death.
YHWH does not let the soul of the righteous go hungry, but he thwarts the craving of the wicked.
A slack hand causes poverty, but the hand of the diligent makes rich.
He who gathers in summer is a wise son, but he who sleeps in harvest is a shameful son.
Blessings are on the head of the righteous, but violence covers the mouth of the wicked.
The memory of the righteous is a blessing, but the name of the wicked will rot.
The wise of heart receives commandments, but a babbling fool will fall.
Whoever walks in integrity walks securely, but he who makes his ways crooked will be found out.
One who winks the eye causes trouble, but a babbling fool will fall.
The mouth of the righteous is a fountain of life, but violence covers the mouth of the wicked.
Hatred stirs up strife, but love covers all offenses.
On the lips of the discerning, wisdom is found, but a rod is for the back of one without heart.
Wise men store up knowledge, but the mouth of the fool invites ruin near.
The rich man’s wealth is his strong city; the ruin of the poor is their poverty.
The wage of the righteous leads to life; the gain of the wicked to sin.
He who heeds instruction is on the path to life, but he who rejects reproof goes astray.
He who conceals hatred has lying lips, and whoever spreads slander is a fool.
When words are many, transgression is not lacking, but whoever restrains his lips is prudent.
The tongue of the righteous is choice silver; the heart of the wicked is of little worth.
The lips of the righteous feed many, but fools die for lack of heart.
The blessing of YHWH makes rich, and he adds no sorrow with it.
Like sport to a fool is doing evil, and wisdom is for a man of understanding.
What the wicked fears will come upon him, but the desire of the righteous will be granted.
When the storm passes, the wicked is no more, but the righteous is an everlasting foundation.
Like vinegar to the teeth and smoke to the eyes, so is the sluggard to those who send him.
The fear of YHWH prolongs days, but the years of the wicked will be shortened.
The hope of the righteous is joy, but the expectation of the wicked perishes.
The way of YHWH is a stronghold to the blameless, but destruction to evildoers.
The righteous will never be removed, but the wicked will not dwell in the land.
The mouth of the righteous brings forth wisdom, but the perverse tongue will be cut off.
The lips of the righteous know what is acceptable, but the mouth of the wicked what is perverse.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 11
מֹאזְנֵי מִרְמָה תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה וְאֶבֶן שְׁלֵמָה רְצוֹנוֹ׃
בָּאָה זָדוֹן וַיָּבוֹא קָלוֹן וְאֶת־צְנוּעִים חָכְמָה׃
תֻּמַּת יְשָׁרִים תַּנְחֵם וְסֶלֶף בּוֹגְדִים יְשַׁדֵּם׃
לֹא־יוֹעִיל הוֹן בְּיוֹם עֶבְרָה וּצְדָקָה תַּצִּיל מִמָּוֶת׃
צִדְקַת תָּמִים תְּיַשֵּׁר דַּרְכּוֹ וּבְרִשְׁעָתוֹ יִפֹּל רָשָׁע׃
צִדְקַת יְשָׁרִים תַּצִּילֵם וּבְהַוַּת בּוֹגְדִים יִלָּכֵדוּ׃
בְּמוֹת אָדָם רָשָׁע תֹּאבַד תִּקְוָה וְתוֹחֶלֶת אֹנִים אָבָדָה׃
צַדִּיק מִצָּרָה נֶחֱלָץ וַיָּבֹא רָשָׁע תַּחְתָּיו׃
בְּפֶה חָנֵף יַשְׁחִית רֵעֵהוּ וּבְדַעַת צַדִּיקִים יֵחָלֵצוּ׃
בְּטוּב צַדִּיקִים תַּעֲלֹץ קִרְיָה וּבַאֲבֹד רְשָׁעִים רִנָּה׃
בְּבִרְכַּת יְשָׁרִים תֵּרוֹם קָרֶת וּבְפִי רְשָׁעִים תֵּהָרֵס׃
בּוֹז לְרֵעֵהוּ חֲסַר־לֵב וְאִישׁ תְּבוּנוֹת יַחֲרִישׁ׃
הוֹלֵךְ רָכִיל מְגַלֶּה סּוֹד וְנֶאֱמַן רוּחַ מְכַסֶּה דָבָר׃
בְּאֵין תַּחְבֻּלוֹת יִפֹּל עָם וּתְשׁוּעָה בְּרֹב יוֹעֵץ׃
רַע־יִרוֹעַ כִּי־עָרַב זָר וְשֹׂנֵא תֹקְעִים בָּטָח׃
חֹנֵן דָּל מַכְבִּיד לוֹ וְשֹׂנֵא מַתָּנֹת יִחְיֶה׃
גֵּמֶל אֵשֶׁת חֵן יִתְמֹךְ כָּבוֹד וְעָרִיצִים יִתְמְכוּ עֹשֶׁר׃
גֹּמֵל נַפְשׁוֹ אִישׁ חָסֶד וְעֹכֵר שְׁאֵרוֹ אַכְזָרִי׃
רְשָׁע עֹשֶׂה פְעֻלַּת שָׁקֶר וְזֹרֵעַ צְדָקָה שֶׂכֶר אֱמֶת׃
כֵּן צְדָקָה לְחַיִּים וּמְרַדֵּף רָעָה לְמוֹתוֹ׃
תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה עִקְּשֵׁי לֵב וּרְצוֹנוֹ תְמִימֵי דָרֶךְ׃
יָד לְיָד לֹא יִנָּקֶה רָע וְזֶרַע צַדִּיקִים נִמְלָט׃
נֶזֶם זָהָב בְּאַף חֲזִיר אִשָּׁה יָפָה וְסָרַת טָעַם׃
תַּאֲוַת צַדִּיקִים רַק־טוֹב תִּקְוַת רְשָׁעִים עֶבְרָה׃
יֵשׁ מְפַזֵּר וְנוֹסָף עוֹד וְחֹשֵׂךְ מִיֹּשֶׁר רַק־לְמַחְסוֹר׃
נֶפֶשׁ בְּרָכָה תְדֻשָּׁן וּמַרְוֶה גַּם־הוּא יוֹרֶה׃
מֹנֵעַ בָּר יִקְּבֻהוּ לְאוֹם וּבְרָכָה לְרֹאשׁ מַשְׁבִּיר׃
שֹׁחֵר טוֹב יְבַקֵּשׁ רָצוֹן וְדֹרֵשׁ רָעָה תְּבוֹאֶנּוּ׃
בּוֹטֵחַ בְּעָשְׁרוֹ הוּא יִפֹּל וְכֶעָלֶה צַדִּיקִים יִפְרָחוּ׃
עֹכֵר בֵּיתוֹ יִנְחַל רוּחַ וְעֶבֶד אֱוִיל לַחֲכַם־לֵב׃
פְּרִי צַדִּיק עֵץ חַיִּים וְלֹקֵחַ נְפָשׁוֹת חָכָם׃
הֵן צַדִּיק בָּאָרֶץ יְשֻׁלָּם אַף כִּי רָשָׁע וְחֹטֵא׃
A false balance is an abomination to YHWH, but a just weight is his delight.
When pride comes, then comes disgrace, but with the humble is wisdom.
The integrity of the upright guides them, but the crookedness of the treacherous destroys them.
Riches do not profit in the day of wrath, but righteousness delivers from death.
The righteousness of the blameless makes his way straight, but the wicked falls by his own wickedness.
The righteousness of the upright delivers them, but the treacherous are taken in their craving.
When a wicked man dies, his hope perishes, and the expectation of strength vanishes.
The righteous is delivered from trouble, and the wicked comes in his place.
With his mouth the hypocrite destroys his neighbor, but through knowledge the righteous are delivered.
When the righteous prosper, the city rejoices, and when the wicked perish there is shouting.
By the blessing of the upright a city is exalted, but by the mouth of the wicked it is overthrown.
Whoever despises his neighbor lacks heart, but a man of understanding keeps silent.
A gossip reveals secrets, but a trustworthy spirit conceals a matter.
Where there is no guidance, a people falls, but in an abundance of counselors there is safety.
Whoever puts up security for a stranger will surely suffer, but one who hates pledges is secure.
A gracious woman gains honor, and ruthless men gain riches.
A kind man benefits his own soul, but the cruel troubles his own flesh.
The wicked earns deceptive wages, but one who sows righteousness gets a sure reward.
Righteousness leads to life, but he who pursues evil pursues his own death.
The perverse in heart are an abomination to YHWH, but those of blameless way are his delight.
Be assured, the evil man will not go unpunished, but the offspring of the righteous will be delivered.
Like a gold ring in a pig’s snout is a beautiful woman without discretion.
The desire of the righteous is only good; the hope of the wicked is wrath.
One gives freely, yet gains even more; another withholds what is right, only to come to poverty.
A generous soul will be enriched, and whoever waters will himself be watered.
The people curse him who withholds grain, but blessing is on the head of him who sells it.
He who diligently seeks good seeks favor, but he who seeks evil, it will come to him.
Whoever trusts in his riches will fall, but the righteous will flourish like a green leaf.
He who troubles his own house will inherit wind, and the fool will be servant to the wise of heart.
The fruit of the righteous is a tree of life, and whoever wins souls is wise.
If the righteous is recompensed on earth, how much more the wicked and the sinner!

>>>>>>> Proverbs 12
אֹהֵב מוּסָר אֹהֵב דָּעַת וְשֹׂנֵא תוֹכַחַת בָּעַר׃
טוֹב יָפִיק רָצוֹן מִיְהוָה וְאִישׁ מְזִמּוֹת יַרְשִׁיעַ׃
לֹא־יִכּוֹן אָדָם בְּרֶשַׁע וְשֹׁרֶשׁ צַדִּיקִים בַּל־יִמּוֹט׃
אֵשֶׁת חַיִל עֲטֶרֶת בַּעְלָהּ וּכְרָקָב בְּעַצְמוֹתָיו מְבִישָׁה׃
מַחְשְׁבוֹת צַדִּיקִים מִשְׁפָּט תַּחְבֻּלוֹת רְשָׁעִים מִרְמָה׃
דִּבְרֵי רְשָׁעִים אֱרָב־דָּם וּפִי יְשָׁרִים יַצִּילֵם׃
הָפֹךְ רְשָׁעִים וְאֵינָם וּבֵית צַדִּיקִים יַעֲמֹד׃
לְפִי־שִׂכְלוֹ יְהֻלַּל־אִישׁ וְנַעֲוֵה־לֵב יִהְיֶה לָבוּז׃
טוֹב נִקְלֶה וְעֶבֶד לוֹ מִמִּתְכַּבֵּד וְחָסֶר־לָחֶם׃
יוֹדֵעַ צַדִּיק נֶפֶשׁ בְּהֶמְתּוֹ וְרַחֲמֵי רְשָׁעִים אַכְזָרִי׃
חֹרֵשׁ אַדְמָתוֹ יִשְׂבַּע לָחֶם וּמְרַדֵּף רֵיקִים חֲסַר־לֵב׃
חָמַד רָשָׁע מְצוֹד רָעִים וְשֹׁרֶשׁ צַדִּיקִים יִתֵּן׃
בְּפֶשַׁע שְׂפָתַיִם מוֹקֵשׁ רָע וַיֵּצֵא מִצָּרָה צַדִּיק׃
מִפְּרִי פִי־אִישׁ יִשְׂבַּע טוֹב וּגְמוּל יְדֵי אָדָם יָשִׁיב לוֹ׃
דֶּרֶךְ אֱוִיל יָשָׁר בְּעֵינָיו וְשֹׁמֵעַ לְעֵצָה חָכָם׃
אֱוִיל בַּיּוֹם יִוָּדַע כַּעְסוֹ וְכֹסֶה קָלוֹן עָרוּם׃
יָפִיחַ אֱמוּנָה יַגִּיד צֶדֶק וְעֵד שְׁקָרִים מִרְמָה׃
יֵשׁ בּוֹטֶה כְּמַדְקְרוֹת חָרֶב וּלְשׁוֹן חֲכָמִים מַרְפֵּא׃
שְׂפַת אֱמֶת תִּכּוֹן לָעַד וְעַד־אַרְגִּיעָה לְשׁוֹן שָׁקֶר׃
מִרְמָה בְּלֵב חֹרְשֵׁי רָע וְלִיעֲצֵי שָׁלוֹם שִׂמְחָה׃
לֹא־יֵאָרַע לַצַּדִּיק כָּל־אָוֶן וּרְשָׁעִים מָלְאוּ רָע׃
תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה שִׂפְתֵי־שָׁקֶר וְעֹשֵׂי אֱמוּנָה רְצוֹנוֹ׃
אָדָם עָרוּם כֹּסֶה דָּעַת וְלֵב כְּסִילִים יִקְרָא אִוֶּלֶת׃
יַד־חָרוּצִים תִּמְשֹׁל וּרְמִיָּה תִּהְיֶה לָמַס׃
דְּאָגָה בְלֶב־אִישׁ יַשְׁחֶנָּה וְדָבָר טוֹב יְשַׂמְּחֶנָּה׃
צַדִּיק יָתוּן לְרֵעֵהוּ וְדֶרֶךְ רְשָׁעִים תַּתְעֵם׃
לֹא־יַחֲרֹךְ רְמִיָּה צֵידוֹ וְהוֹן אָדָם יָקָר חָרוּץ׃
בְּאֹרַח צְדָקָה חַיִּים וְדֶרֶךְ נְתִיבָה אַל־מָוֶת׃
Whoever loves discipline loves knowledge, but he who hates reproof is stupid.
A good man obtains favor from YHWH, but a man of evil plans he condemns.
A man will not be established by wickedness, but the root of the righteous will not be moved.
An excellent wife is the crown of her husband, but she who brings shame is like rottenness in his bones.
The thoughts of the righteous are just; the schemes of the wicked are deceit.
The words of the wicked lie in wait for blood, but the mouth of the upright delivers them.
The wicked are overthrown and are no more, but the house of the righteous will stand.
A man is praised according to his wisdom, but the twisted of heart will be despised.
Better is one who is lightly esteemed and has a servant than one who honors himself and lacks bread.
The righteous cares for the life of his animal, but the mercy of the wicked is cruel.
Whoever works his land will have plenty of bread, but he who follows worthless pursuits lacks sense.
The wicked covets the spoil of evil men, but the root of the righteous yields fruit.
In the transgression of the lips is a snare, but the righteous will escape trouble.
From the fruit of a man’s mouth he is satisfied with good, and the work of a man’s hands will return to him.
The way of a fool is right in his own eyes, but a wise man listens to counsel.
A fool shows his anger immediately, but a prudent man ignores an insult.
Whoever speaks truth declares righteousness, but a false witness deceit.
There is one who speaks like the piercing of a sword, but the tongue of the wise brings healing.
Truthful lips endure forever, but a lying tongue is only for a moment.
Deceit is in the heart of those who devise evil, but those who plan peace have joy.
No harm befalls the righteous, but the wicked are filled with trouble.
Lying lips are an abomination to YHWH, but those who act faithfully are his delight.
A prudent man conceals knowledge, but the heart of fools proclaims folly.
The hand of the diligent will rule, but laziness will be forced labor.
Anxiety in a man’s heart weighs him down, but a good word makes him glad.
The righteous is a guide to his neighbor, but the way of the wicked leads them astray.
No deceitful hunter catches his prey, but the wealth of a diligent man is precious.
In the path of righteousness is life, and in its pathway there is no death.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 13
בֵּן חָכָם מוּסַר אָב וְלֵץ לֹא־שָׁמַע גְּעָרָה׃
מִפְּרִי פִי־אִישׁ יֹאכַל טוֹב וְנֶפֶשׁ בֹּגְדִים חָמָס׃
נֹצֵר פִּיו שֹׁמֵר נַפְשׁוֹ פֹּשֵׂק שְׂפָתָיו מְחִתָּה־לוֹ׃
מִתְאַוֶּה וָאַיִן נַפְשׁוֹ עָצֵל וְנֶפֶשׁ חָרוּצִים תְּדֻשָּׁן׃
דְּבַר־שֶׁקֶר יִשְׂנָא צַדִּיק וְרָשָׁע יַבְאִישׁ וְיַחְפִּיר׃
צְדָקָה תִּצֹּר תָּם־דָּרֶךְ וְרִשְׁעָה תְסַלֵּף חַטָּאת׃
יֵשׁ מִתְעַשֵּׁר וְאֵין כֹּל מִתְרוֹשֵׁשׁ וְהוֹן רָב׃
כֹּפֶר נֶפֶשׁ־אִישׁ עָשְׁרוֹ וְרָשׁ לֹא שָׁמַע גְּעָרָה׃
אוֹר צַדִּיקִים יִשְׂמָח וְנֵר רְשָׁעִים יִדְעָךְ׃
רַק־בְּזָדוֹן יִתֵּן מַצּוֹת וְאֵת נוֹעָצִים חָכְמָה׃
הוֹן מֵהֶבֶל יִמְעָט וְקֹבֵץ עַל־יָד יַרְבֶּה׃
תּוֹחֶלֶת מְמֻשָּׁכָה מַחֲלָה־לֵב וְעֵץ חַיִּים תַּאֲוָה בָאָה׃
בָּזוֹת לְבָרָה מַאֲכָלָה וְעֵץ חַיִּים תַּאֲוָה בָאָה׃
מִצְוַת חָכָם מְקוֹר חַיִּים לָסוּר מִמֹּקְשֵׁי מָוֶת׃
שֵׂכֶל טוֹב יִתֵּן חֵן וְדֶרֶךְ בֹּגְדִים אֵיתָן׃
כָּל־עָרוּם יַעֲשֶׂה בְדָעַת וּכְסִיל יִפְרֹשׂ אִוֶּלֶת׃
מַלְאָךְ רָשָׁע יִפֹּל בְּרָעָה וְצִיר אֱמוּנִים מַרְפֵּא׃
רֵישׁ וְקָלוֹן פֹּרֵעַ מוּסָר וְשֹׁמֵר תּוֹכַחַת יְכֻבָּד׃
תַּאֲוָה נִהְיָה תַּעֲרֵב לָנָפֶשׁ וְתוֹעֲבַת כְּסִילִים סוּר מֵרָע׃
הוֹלֵךְ אֶת־חֲכָמִים יֶחְכָּם וְרֹעֶה כְסִילִים יֵרוֹעַ׃
רָע יִרְדֹּף חַטָּאִים וְלַצַּדִּיקִים יְשַׁלֶּם־טוֹב׃
טוֹב יַנְחִיל בְּנֵי בָנִים וְצָפוּן לַצַּדִּיק חֵיל חוֹטֵא׃
רָב־אָכֶל נִיר רָאשִׁים וְיֵשׁ נִסְחָף בְּלֹא־מִשְׁפָּט׃
חוֹשֵׂךְ שִׁבְטוֹ שׂוֹנֵא בְנוֹ וְאֹהֲבוֹ שִׁחֲרוֹ מוּסָר׃
צַדִּיק אֹכֵל לְשֹׂבַע נַפְשׁוֹ וּבֶטֶן רְשָׁעִים תֶּחְסָר׃
A wise son hears his father’s instruction, but a scoffer does not listen to rebuke.
From the fruit of a man’s mouth he eats what is good, but the desire of the treacherous is violence.
Whoever guards his mouth preserves his life; he who opens wide his lips comes to ruin.
The soul of the sluggard craves and gets nothing, but the soul of the diligent is richly supplied.
The righteous hates falsehood, but the wicked brings shame and disgrace.
Righteousness guards him whose way is blameless, but wickedness overthrows the sinner.
One pretends to be rich yet has nothing; another pretends to be poor yet has great wealth.
The ransom of a man’s life is his wealth, but the poor does not hear rebuke.
The light of the righteous rejoices, but the lamp of the wicked is put out.
By insolence comes nothing but strife, but with those who take advice is wisdom.
Wealth gained hastily will dwindle, but whoever gathers little by little will increase it.
Hope deferred makes the heart sick, but a desire fulfilled is a tree of life.
Whoever despises the word brings destruction on himself, but he who fears the commandment will be rewarded.
The teaching of the wise is a fountain of life, that one may turn away from the snares of death.
Good sense wins favor, but the way of the treacherous is hard.
Every prudent man acts with knowledge, but a fool flaunts his folly.
A wicked messenger falls into trouble, but a faithful envoy brings healing.
Poverty and disgrace come to him who ignores instruction, but he who heeds reproof is honored.
Desire fulfilled is sweet to the soul, but it is an abomination to fools to turn away from evil.
Whoever walks with the wise becomes wise, but the companion of fools suffers harm.
Disaster pursues sinners, but the righteous are rewarded with good.
A good man leaves an inheritance to his children’s children, but the sinner’s wealth is laid up for the righteous.
Abundant food is in the fallow ground of the poor, but it is swept away by injustice.
Whoever spares the rod hates his son, but he who loves him is diligent to discipline him.
The righteous eats to the satisfying of his soul, but the belly of the wicked suffers lack.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 14
חַכְמוֹת נָשִׁים בָּנְתָה בֵיתָהּ וְאִוֶּלֶת בְּיָדֶיהָ תֶהֶרְסֶנּוּ׃
הוֹלֵךְ בְּיָשְׁרוֹ יְרֵא יְהוָה וּנְלוֹז דְּרָכָיו בּוֹזֵהוּ׃
בְּפִי אֱוִיל חֹטֶר גַּאֲוָה וּשְׂפָתֵי חֲכָמִים תִּשְׁמוּרֵם׃
בְּאֵין אֲלָפִים אֵבוּס בָּר וְרָב תְּבוּאוֹת בְּכֹחַ שׁוֹר׃
עֵד אֱמוּנִים לֹא יְכַזֵּב וְיָפִיחַ כְּזָבִים עֵד שָׁקֶר׃
בִּקַּשׁ לֵץ חָכְמָה וָאַיִן וְדַעַת לְנָבוֹן נָקָל׃
לֵךְ מִנֶּגֶד לְאִישׁ כְּסִיל וּבַל־יָדַעְתָּ שִׂפְתֵי דָעַת׃
חָכְמַת עָרוּם הָבִין דַּרְכּוֹ וְאִוֶּלֶת כְּסִילִים מִרְמָה׃
אֱוִלִים יָלִיץ אָשָׁם וּבֵין יְשָׁרִים רָצוֹן׃
לֵב יוֹדֵעַ מָרַת נַפְשׁוֹ וּבְשִׂמְחָתוֹ לֹא־יִתְעָרַב זָר׃
בֵּית רְשָׁעִים יִשָּׁמֵד וְאֹהֶל יְשָׁרִים יַפְרִיחַ׃
יֵשׁ דֶּרֶךְ יָשָׁר לִפְנֵי־אִישׁ וְאַחֲרִיתָהּ דַּרְכֵי מָוֶת׃
גַּם־בִּשְׂחוֹק יִכְאַב־לֵב וְאַחֲרִית שִׂמְחָה תּוּגָה׃
מִדְּרָכָיו יִשְׂבַּע סוּג לֵב וּמֵעָלָיו אִישׁ טוֹב׃
פֶּתִי יַאֲמִין לְכָל־דָּבָר וְעָרוּם יָבִין לַאֲשֻׁרוֹ׃
חָכָם יָרֵא וְסָר מֵרָע וּכְסִיל מִתְעַבֵּר וּבוֹטֵחַ׃
קַל לַעֲשׂוֹת אִוֶּלֶת וְאִישׁ מְזִמּוֹת יִשָּׂנֵא׃
חֲסִידִים יִנְחֲלוּ־טוֹב וּמְצֹרִים יַנְחִלוּ רָע׃
פְּתָאִים נָחֲלוּ אִוֶּלֶת וַעֲרוּמִים יַכְתִּירוּ דָעַת׃
רָעִים יִשְׁתַּחֲווּ לִפְנֵי־טוֹבִים וּרְשָׁעִים עַל־שַׁעֲרֵי צַדִּיק׃
גַּם־לְרֵעֵהוּ יִשָּׂנֵא רָשׁ וְאֹהֲבֵי עָשִׁיר רַבִּים׃
בָּז לְרֵעֵהוּ חוֹטֵא וּמְחֹנֵן עֲנָיִים אַשְׁרָיו׃
הֲלוֹא יִתְעָם מְחַשְּׁבֵי רָע וְחֶסֶד וֶאֱמֶת לְמַחֲשְׁבֵי טוֹב׃
בְּכָל־עֶצֶב יִהְיֶה מוֹתָר וּדְבַר־שְׂפָתַיִם רַק־לְמַחְסוֹר׃
עֲטֶרֶת חֲכָמִים עָשְׁרָם אִוֶּלֶת כְּסִילִים אִוֶּלֶת׃
מוֹצִיא דְבָרִים יְאֻמַּן וְעֵד שְׁקָרִים מִרְמָה׃
בְּיִרְאַת יְהוָה מִבְטַח עֹז וּלְבָנָיו יִהְיֶה מַחְסֶה׃
יִרְאַת יְהוָה מְקוֹר חַיִּים לָסוּר מִמֹּקְשֵׁי מָוֶת׃
בְּרֹב עָם הַדְרַת־מֶלֶךְ וּבְאֶפֶס לְאֹם מְחִתַּת רָזוֹן׃
אֶרֶךְ אַפַּיִם רַב־תְּבוּנָה וּקְצַר־רוּחַ מֵרִים אִוֶּלֶת׃
חַיֵּי בְשָׂרִים לֵב מַרְפֵּא וּרְקַב עֲצָמוֹת קִנְאָה׃
עֹשֵׁק דָּל חֵרֵף עֹשֵׂהוּ וּמְכַבְּדוֹ חֹנֵן אֶבְיוֹן׃
בְּרָעָתוֹ יִדָּחֶה רָשָׁע וְחֹסֶה בְמוֹתוֹ צַדִּיק׃
Wisdoms build her house, but folly tears it down with her own hands.
He who walks in uprightness fears YHWH, but he who is crooked in his ways despises him.
In the mouth of the fool is a rod of pride, but the lips of the wise preserve them.
Where there are no oxen, the manger is clean, but abundant harvest is by the strength of the ox.
A faithful witness does not lie, but a false witness breathes lies.
A scoffer seeks wisdom and finds none, but knowledge is easy for the discerning.
Go away from a foolish man; you will not find knowledge on his lips.
The wisdom of the prudent is to discern his way, but the folly of fools is deceit.
Fools mock at guilt, but among the upright there is favor.
The heart knows its own bitterness, and no stranger shares its joy.
The house of the wicked will be destroyed, but the tent of the upright will flourish.
There is a way that seems right to a man, but its end is the way of death.
Even in laughter the heart may ache, and the end of joy may be grief.
The backslider in heart will be filled with his own ways, but a good man will be satisfied from above.
The simple believes everything, but the prudent considers his steps.
A wise man is cautious and turns away from evil, but a fool is reckless and confident.
One who is quick to anger acts foolishly, and a man of evil devices is hated.
The simple inherit folly, but the prudent are crowned with knowledge.
The evil bow down before the good, and the wicked at the gates of the righteous.
The poor is disliked even by his neighbor, but many are those who love the rich.
Whoever despises his neighbor sins, but he who is kind to the poor is blessed.
Do they not go astray who devise evil, but steadfast love and faithfulness belong to those who plan good?
In all toil there is profit, but mere talk leads only to poverty.
The crown of the wise is their riches, but the folly of fools is folly.
A truthful witness saves lives, but one who breathes lies is deceitful.
In the fear of YHWH there is strong confidence, and his children will have refuge.
The fear of YHWH is a fountain of life, turning one away from the snares of death.
In a multitude of people is the glory of a king, but without people a ruler is ruined.
Whoever is slow to anger has great understanding, but he who is quick-tempered exalts folly.
A tranquil heart gives life to the flesh, but envy makes the bones rot.
Whoever oppresses the poor insults his Maker, but he who is generous to the needy honors him.
In his disaster the wicked is overthrown, but the righteous has a refuge in his death.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 15
מַעֲנֶה־רַךְ יָשִׁיב חֵמָה וּדְבַר־עֶצֶב יַעֲלֶה־אָף׃
לְשׁוֹן חֲכָמִים תֵּיטִיב דָּעַת וּפִי כְסִילִים יַבִּיעַ אִוֶּלֶת׃
בְּכָל־מָקוֹם עֵינֵי יְהוָה צֹפֲתוֹת רָעִים וְטוֹבִים׃
מַרְפֵּא לָשׁוֹן עֵץ חַיִּים וְסֶלֶף בָּהּ שֶׁבֶר בְּרוּחַ׃
אֱוִיל יִנְאַץ מוּסַר אָב וְשֹׁמֵר תּוֹכַחַת יַעְרִים׃
בֵּית צַדִּיק חֹסֶן רָב וּבִתְבוּאַת רָשָׁע נֶעְכָּרֶת׃
שִׂפְתֵי חֲכָמִים יְזָרוּ דָּעַת וְלֵב כְּסִילִים לֹא־כֵן׃
זֶבַח רְשָׁעִים תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה וּתְפִלַּת יְשָׁרִים רְצוֹנוֹ׃
תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה דֶּרֶךְ רָשָׁע וּמְרַדֵּף צְדָקָה יֶאֱהָב׃
מוּסָר רָע לְעֹזֵב אֹרַח שׂוֹנֵא תוֹכַחַת יָמוּת׃
שְׁאוֹל וַאֲבַדּוֹן נֶגֶד יְהוָה אַף כִּי לִבּוֹת בְּנֵי־אָדָם׃
לֹא־יֶאֱהַב לֵץ הוֹכֵחַ לוֹ אֶל־חֲכָמִים לֹא יֵלֵךְ׃
לֵב שָׂמֵחַ יֵיטִב פָּנִים וּבְעַצְּבַת לֵב רוּחַ נְכֵאָה׃
לֵב נָבוֹן יְבַקֶּשׁ דָּעַת וּפְנֵי כְסִילִים יִרְעוּ אִוֶּלֶת׃
כָּל־יְמֵי עָנִי רָעִים וְטוֹב לֵב מִשְׁתֶּה תָמִיד׃
טוֹב מְעַט בְּיִרְאַת יְהוָה מֵאוֹצָר רָב וּמְהוּמָה בּוֹ׃
טוֹב אֲרֻחַת יָרָק וְאַהֲבָה שָׁם מִשּׁוֹר אָבוּס וְשִׂנְאָה בּוֹ׃
אִישׁ חֵמָה יְגָרֶה מָדוֹן וְאֶרֶךְ אַפַּיִם יַשְׁקִיט רִיב׃
דֶּרֶךְ עָצֵל כִּמְשׂוּכַת חָדֶק וְאֹרַח יְשָׁרִים סְלֻלָה׃
בֵּן חָכָם יְשַׂמַּח אָב וּכְסִיל אָדָם בוֹזֶה אִמּוֹ׃
אִוֶּלֶת שִׂמְחָה לַחֲסַר־לֵב וְאִישׁ תְּבוּנָה יְיַשֵּׁר לָכֶת׃
בְּאֵין הַחֲרָצִים יִפֹּל עָם וְתְשׁוּעָה בְּרֹב יוֹעֵץ׃
שִׂמְחָה לָאִישׁ בְּמַעֲנֵה פִיו וְדָבָר בְּעִתּוֹ מַה־טּוֹב׃
אֹרַח חַיִּים לְמַעְלָה לְמַשְׂכִּיל לְמַעַן סוּר מִשְּׁאוֹל מָטָּה׃
A soft answer turns away wrath, but a harsh word stirs up anger.
The tongue of the wise commends knowledge, but the mouth of fools pours out folly.
In every place the eyes of YHWH are watching evil and good.
A healing tongue is a tree of life, but perverseness in it breaks the spirit.
A fool despises his father’s instruction, but he who keeps reproof is prudent.
The house of the righteous has great treasure, but the income of the wicked is troubled.
The lips of the wise spread knowledge, but the heart of fools is not so.
The sacrifice of the wicked is an abomination to YHWH, but the prayer of the upright is his delight.
The way of the wicked is an abomination to YHWH, but he loves one who pursues righteousness.
Severe discipline is for him who forsakes the way; whoever hates reproof will die.
Sheol and Abaddon lie open before YHWH—how much more the hearts of men!
A scoffer does not love one who corrects him, nor will he go to the wise.
A glad heart makes a cheerful face, but by sorrow of heart the spirit is crushed.
The heart of the discerning seeks knowledge, but the mouth of fools feeds on folly.
All the days of the afflicted are evil, but the cheerful heart has a continual feast.
Better is a little with the fear of YHWH than great treasure and turmoil with it.
Better is a dinner of herbs where love is than a fattened ox and hatred with it.
A wrathful man stirs up strife, but one who is slow to anger quiets contention.
The way of the sluggard is like a hedge of thorns, but the path of the upright is a highway.
A wise son makes a father glad, but a foolish man despises his mother.
Folly is joy to him who lacks sense, but a man of understanding walks straight.
Without counsel plans fail, but with many advisers they succeed.
A man has joy in the answer of his mouth, and a word in season, how good it is!
The path of life leads upward for the prudent, that he may turn away from Sheol below.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 16
לְאָדָם מַעַרְכֵי־לֵב וּמֵיְהוָה מַעֲנֵה לָשׁוֹן׃
כָּל־דַּרְכֵי־אִישׁ זַךְ בְּעֵינָיו וְתֹכֵן רוּחוֹת יְהוָה׃
גֹּל אֶל־יְהוָה מַעֲשֶׂיךָ וְיִכֹּנוּ מַחְשְׁבֹתֶיךָ׃
כֹּל פָּעַל יְהוָה לְמַעֲנֵהוּ וְגַם־רָשָׁע לְיוֹם רָעָה׃
תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה כָּל־גְּבַהּ־לֵב יָד לְיָד לֹא יִנָּקֶה׃
בְּחֶסֶד וֶאֱמֶת יְכֻפַּר עָוֹן וּבְיִרְאַת יְהוָה סוּר מֵרָע׃
בִּרְצוֹת יְהוָה דַּרְכֵי־אִישׁ גַּם־אוֹיְבָיו יַשְׁלִים אִתּוֹ׃
טוֹב מְעַט בִּצְדָקָה מֵרֹב תְּבוּאוֹת בְּלֹא מִשְׁפָּט׃
לֵב אָדָם יְחַשֵּׁב דַּרְכּוֹ וַיהוָה יָכִין צַעֲדוֹ׃
קֶסֶם עַל־שִׂפְתֵי־מֶלֶךְ בְּמִשְׁפָּט לֹא יִמְעַל פִּיו׃
פֶּלֶס וּמֹאזְנֵי מִשְׁפָּט לַיהוָה מַעֲשֵׂהוּ כָּל־אַבְנֵי כִּיס׃
תּוֹעֲבַת מְלָכִים עֲשׂוֹת רֶשַׁע כִּי בִצְדָקָה יִכּוֹן כִּסֵּא׃
רְצוֹן מְלָכִים שִׂפְתֵי־צֶדֶק וְדֹבֵר יְשָׁרִים יֶאֱהָב׃
חֲמַת־מֶלֶךְ מַלְאֲכֵי־מָוֶת וְאִישׁ חָכָם יְכַפְּרֶנָּה׃
בְּאוֹר־פְּנֵי־מֶלֶךְ חַיִּים וּרְצוֹנוֹ כְּעָב מַלְקוֹשׁ׃
טוֹב לִקְחַת נִדְבָּה מִכֶּסֶף וּמִזָּהָב חֵן בְּעֵינֵי אֱלֹהִים׃
מְסִלַּת יְשָׁרִים סוּר מֵרָע שֹׁמֵר נַפְשׁוֹ נֹצֵר דַּרְכּוֹ׃
לִפְנֵי־שֶׁבֶר גָּאוֹן וְלִפְנֵי כִשָּׁלוֹן גֹּבַהּ־רוּחַ׃
טוֹב שְׁפַל־רוּחַ אֶת־עֲנָוִים מֵחַלֵּק שָׁלָל אֶת־גֵּאִים׃
מַשְׂכִּיל עַל־דָּבָר יִמְצָא טוֹב וּבוֹטֵחַ בַּיהוָה אַשְׁרָיו׃
חָכַם לֵב יִקָּח מִצְוֹת וֶאֱוִיל שְׂפָתַיִם יִלָּבֵט׃
פֶּתִי יַאֲמִין לְכָל־דָּבָר וְעָרוּם יָבִין לַאֲשֻׁרוֹ׃
מְזִמַּת אִוֶּלֶת חַטָּאת וְתוֹעֲבַת לֵץ בִּירְאַת אֱלֹהִים׃
כִּי בְיִרְאַת יְהוָה מִבְטַח עֹז וְלִבְנֵיהֶם יִהְיֶה מַחְסֶה׃
תּוֹחֶלֶת צַדִּיקִים שִׂמְחָה וְתִקְוַת רְשָׁעִים תֹּאבֵד׃
עֵץ חַיִּים תַּאֲוָה בָאָה וְסָר מֵרָע שֹׂנֵא נַפְשׁוֹ׃
אִישׁ בְּלִיַּעַל כֹּרֶה רָע וְעַל־שְׂפָתָיו כְּאֵשׁ צָרָבֶת׃
אִישׁ תַּהְפֻּכוֹת יְשַׁלַּח מָדוֹן וְנִרְגָּן מַפְרִיד אַלּוּף׃
אִישׁ חָמָס יְפַתֶּה רֵעֵהוּ וְהוֹלִיכוֹ בְּדֶרֶךְ לֹא־טוֹב׃
עֹצֶה עֵינָיו לַחְשֹׁב תַּהְפֻּכוֹת קֹרֵץ שְׂפָתָיו כִּלָּה רָעָה׃
עֲטֶרֶת תִּפְאֶרֶת שֵׂיבָה בְּדֶרֶךְ צְדָקָה תִּמָּצֵא׃
טוֹב אֶרֶךְ אַפַּיִם מִגִּבּוֹר וּמֹשֵׁל בְּרוּחוֹ מִלֹּכֵד עִיר׃
בְּחֵיק יֻטַּל אֶת־הַגּוֹרָל וּמֵיְהוָה כָּל־מִשְׁפָּטוֹ׃
To man belong the plans of the heart, but from YHWH comes the answer of the tongue.
All a man’s ways are pure in his own eyes, but YHWH weighs the spirits.
Commit your works to YHWH, and your plans will be established.
YHWH has made everything for its purpose, even the wicked for the day of trouble.
Everyone proud in heart is an abomination to YHWH; he will not go unpunished.
By steadfast love and faithfulness iniquity is atoned, and by the fear of YHWH one turns from evil.
When a man’s ways please YHWH, he makes even his enemies to be at peace with him.
Better is a little with righteousness than great revenues without justice.
The heart of man plans his way, but YHWH establishes his steps.
Divination is on the lips of the king; his mouth does not err in judgment.
Honest weights and scales are YHWH’s; all the weights in the bag are his work.
It is an abomination for kings to do evil, for a throne is established by righteousness.
Righteous lips are the delight of kings, and they love him who speaks what is right.
The wrath of a king is a messenger of death, but a wise man will appease it.
In the light of the king’s face is life, and his favor is like the cloud of the latter rain.
How much better to get wisdom than gold, to get understanding rather than silver.
The highway of the upright turns aside from evil; whoever guards his way preserves his life.
Pride goes before destruction, and a haughty spirit before a fall.
Better to be of a lowly spirit with the humble than to divide spoil with the proud.
Whoever gives thought to the word will discover good, and blessed is he who trusts in YHWH.
The wise of heart is called discerning, and sweetness of speech increases persuasiveness.
The path of the upright is to turn from evil; he who guards his way preserves his soul.
Pride in heart is an abomination to YHWH; though they join forces, none will go unpunished.
By steadfast love and faithfulness iniquity is atoned, and by the fear of YHWH one turns from evil.
The desire of the righteous ends only in good; the expectation of the wicked is wrath.
There is a way that seems right to a man, but its end is the way to death.
A worthless man digs up evil, and on his lips is like a scorching fire.
A perverse man spreads strife, and a whisperer separates close friends.
A violent man entices his neighbor and leads him in a way that is not good.
He who winks his eyes plans deceit; he who purses his lips brings evil to pass.
Gray hair is a crown of glory; it is gained in a righteous life.
Whoever is slow to anger is better than the mighty, and he who rules his spirit than he who takes a city.
The lot is cast into the lap, but its every decision is from YHWH.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 17
טוֹב פַּת חֲרֵבָה וְשַׁלְוָה בָּהּ מִבַּיִת מָלֵא זִבְחֵי רִיב׃
עֶבֶד מַשְׂכִּיל יִמְשֹׁל בְּבֵן מֵבִישׁ וּבְתוֹךְ אַחִים יַחֲלֹק נַחֲלָה׃
מַצְרֵף לַכֶּסֶף וְכוּר לַזָּהָב וּבֹחֵן לִבּוֹת יְהוָה׃
מֵרַע מַקְשִׁיב עַל־שְׂפַת אָוֶן שֶׁקֶר מֵזִין לְשׁוֹן הַוּוֹת׃
לֵעֵג לָרָשׁ חֵרֵף עֹשֵׂהוּ שָׂמֵחַ לְאֵיד לֹא יִנָּקֶה׃
עֲטֶרֶת זְקֵנִים בְּנֵי בָנִים וְתִפְאֶרֶת בָּנִים אֲבוֹתָם׃
לֹא נָאוֶה לִנְבָל שְׂפַת־יֶתֶר אַף כִּי־לְנָדִיב שְׂפַת שָׁקֶר׃
אֶבֶן חֵן הַשֹּׁחַד בְּעֵינֵי בְעָלָיו אֶל כָּל אֲשֶׁר יִפְנֶה יַשְׂכִּיל׃
מְכַסֶּה פֶּשַׁע מְבַקֵּשׁ אַהֲבָה וְשֹׁנֶה בְדָבָר מַפְרִיד אַלּוּף׃
תַּחַת גְּעָרָה בְּמֵבִין מֵהַכּוֹת כְּסִיל מֵאָה׃
רַק מְרִי יְבַקֶּשׁ רָע וּמַלְאָךְ אַכְזָר יְשֻׁלַּח־בּוֹ׃
פֶּגַע דֹּב שַׁכּוּל וְאַל כְּסִיל בְּאִוַּלְתּוֹ׃
מֵשִׁיב רָעָה תַּחַת טוֹבָה לֹא־תָמוּשׁ רָעָה מִבֵּיתוֹ׃
פֹּטֵר מַיִם רֵאשִׁית מָדוֹן וְלִפְנֵי הִתְגַּלֵּעַ הָרִיב נְטוֹשׁ׃
מַצְדִּיק רָשָׁע וּמַרְשִׁיעַ צַדִּיק תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה גַּם־שְׁנֵיהֶם׃
לָמָּה־זֶּה מְחִיר בְּיַד־כְּסִיל לִקְנוֹת חָכְמָה וְלֵב אֵין׃
בְּכָל־עֵת אֹהֵב הָרֵעַ וְאָח לְצָרָה יִוָּלֵד׃
אִישׁ תְּבוּנָה יַחְסֹר דָּעַת וּכְסִיל יִתְעַרֵב לֵב׃
לֹא־טוֹב פְּנֵי־רָשָׁע לָקַחַת שֹׁחַד לְהַטּוֹת אָרְחוֹת מִשְׁפָּט׃
נָכוֹן מֵרֵאשִׁית מָדוֹן וְהַנִּגָּלֶה רִיב נָשָׁא׃
אִישׁ חֲסַר־לֵב תּוֹקֵעַ כָּף עֹרֵב עֲרֻבָּה לִפְנֵי רֵעֵהוּ׃
אֹהֵב פֶּשַׁע אֹהֵב מַצְדִּיק לֵץ וּמְגַלֶּה סוֹד מַפְרִיד אַלּוּף׃
אִישׁ עָקֵשׁ לֵב לֹא־יִמְצָא טוֹב וְנֶהְפָּךְ לְשׁוֹנוֹ יִפֹּל בְּרָעָה׃
יֹלֵד כְּסִיל לְתֻגָּה לוֹ וְלֹא־יִשְׂמַח אֲבִי נָבָל׃
לֵב שָׂמֵחַ יֵיטִב גֵּהָה וְרוּחַ נְכֵאָה תְּיַבֶּשׁ גָּרֶם׃
שֹׁחֵד מֵחֵיק רָשָׁע יִקָּח לְהַטּוֹת אֹרְחוֹת מִשְׁפָּט׃
לִפְנֵי נֶגֶד תּוֹבָנָה חָכְמָה וְעֵינֵי כְסִיל בִּקְצֵה־אָרֶץ׃
לֵץ אֵינֶנּוּ חָפֵץ בִּתְבוּנָה כִּי אִם־בְּהִתְגַּלּוֹת לִבּוֹ׃
בְּבוֹא רָשָׁע בָּא גַּם־בּוּז וְעִם קָלוֹן חֶרְפָּה׃
מַצְדִּיק רָשָׁע וּמַרְשִׁיעַ צַדִּיק תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה גַּם־שְׁנֵיהֶם׃
Better is a dry morsel with quiet than a house full of feasting and strife.
A servant who deals wisely will rule over a son who acts shamefully, and will share the inheritance among the brothers.
The refining pot is for silver, and the furnace for gold, but YHWH tests hearts.
An evildoer listens to wicked lips; a liar gives ear to a destructive tongue.
Whoever mocks the poor insults his Maker; he who is glad at calamity will not go unpunished.
Grandchildren are the crown of the aged, and the glory of children is their fathers.
Fine speech is not fitting for a fool, much less false speech for a noble.
A bribe is like a magic stone in the eyes of its owner; wherever he turns he prospers.
Whoever covers an offense seeks love, but he who repeats a matter separates close friends.
A rebuke goes deeper into a man of understanding than a hundred blows into a fool.
An evil man seeks only rebellion, and a cruel messenger will be sent against him.
Let a bear robbed of her cubs meet a man rather than a fool in his folly.
Whoever returns evil for good, evil will not depart from his house.
The beginning of strife is like letting out water, so quit before the quarrel breaks out.
He who justifies the wicked and he who condemns the righteous are both an abomination to YHWH.
Why should a fool have money in his hand to buy wisdom when he has no sense?
A friend loves at all times, and a brother is born for adversity.
A man lacking sense gives pledges and puts up security in the presence of his neighbor.
Whoever loves transgression loves strife; whoever builds a high gate seeks destruction.
A crooked heart does not find good, and one with a twisted tongue falls into calamity.
He who sires a fool gets grief for it, and the father of a fool has no joy.
A joyful heart is good medicine, but a crushed spirit dries up the bones.
A bribe from the bosom of the wicked perverts the ways of justice.
The discerning sets his face toward wisdom, but the eyes of a fool are on the ends of the earth.
A foolish son brings grief to his father and bitterness to her who bore him.
It is not good to fine the righteous, or to strike the noble for their uprightness.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 18
לְתַאֲוָה יְבַקֵּשׁ נִפְרָד בְּכָל־תּוּשִׁיָּה יִתְגַּלָּע׃
לֹא יַחְפֹּץ כְּסִיל בִּתְבוּנָה כִּי אִם־בְּהִתְגַּלּוֹת לִבּוֹ׃
בְּבוֹא רָשָׁע בָּא גַּם־בּוּז וְעִם קָלוֹן חֶרְפָּה׃
מַיִם עֲמֻקִּים דִּבְרֵי פִי־אִישׁ נַחַל נֹבֵעַ מְקוֹר חָכְמָה׃
שְׂאֵת פְּנֵי רָשָׁע לֹא־טוֹב לְהַטּוֹת צַדִּיק בַּמִּשְׁפָּט׃
שִׂפְתֵי כְסִיל יָבֹאוּ בְרִיב וּפִיו לְמַהֲלֻמוֹת יִקְרָא׃
פִּי־כְסִיל מְחִתָּה־לוֹ וּשְׂפָתָיו מוֹקֵשׁ נַפְשׁוֹ׃
דִּבְרֵי נִרְגָּן כְּמִתְלַהֲמִים וְהֵם יָרְדוּ חַדְרֵי־בָטֶן׃
גַּם מִתְרַפֶּה בִמְלַאכְתּוֹ אָח הוּא לְבַעַל מַשְׁחִית׃
מִגְדַּל־עֹז שֵׁם יְהוָה בּוֹ יָרוּץ צַדִּיק וְנִשְׂגָּב׃
הוֹן עָשִׁיר קִרְיַת עֻזּוֹ וּכְחוֹמָה נִשְׂגָּבָה בְּמַשְׂכִּיתוֹ׃
לִפְנֵי־שֶׁבֶר יִגְבַּהּ לֵב־אִישׁ וְלִפְנֵי כָבוֹד עֲנָוָה׃
מֵשִׁיב דָּבָר בְּטֶרֶם יִשְׁמַע אִוֶּלֶת הִיא־לוֹ וּכְלִמָּה׃
רוּחַ־אִישׁ יְכַלְכֵּל מַחֲלֵהוּ וְרוּחַ נְכֵאָה מִי יִשָּׂאֶנָּה׃
לֵב נָבוֹן יִקְנֶה־דָּעַת וְאֹזֶן חֲכָמִים תְּבַקֶּשׁ דָּעַת׃
מַתָּן אָדָם יַרְחִיב לוֹ וְלִפְנֵי גְדֹלִים יַנְחֶנּוּ׃
צַדִּיק רִאשׁוֹן בְּרִיבוֹ יָבֹא רֵעֵהוּ וַחֲקָרוֹ׃
חַכְמַת עָרוּם תָּבוֹא־בַדָּעַת וְאָזְנֵי חֲכָמִים תְּבַקֵּשׁ דָּעַת׃
מַתָּן אָדָם יַרְחִיב לוֹ וְלִפְנֵי גְדֹלִים יַנְחֶנּוּ׃
גּוֹרָל יַשְׁבִּית מְרִיבוֹת וּבֵין עֲצוּמִים יַפְרִיד׃
אָח נִפְשָׁע מִקִּרְיַת עֹז וּמִדּוֹנֵי בְרִיחַ אַרְמוֹן׃
מִפְּרִי פִי־אִישׁ תִּשְׂבַּע בִּטְנוֹ תְּבוּאַת שְׂפָתָיו יִשְׂבָּע׃
מָוֶת וְחַיִּים בְּיַד־לָשׁוֹן וְאֹהֲבֶיהָ יֹאכַל פִּרְיָהּ׃
מָצָא אִשָּׁה מָצָא טוֹב וַיָּפֶק רָצוֹן מֵיְהוָה׃
רָשׁ יְדַבֵּר תַּחֲנוּנִים וְעָשִׁיר יַעֲנֶה עַזּוֹת׃
אִישׁ רֵעִים לְהִתְרֹעֵעַ וְיֵשׁ אֹהֵב דָּבֵק מֵאָח׃
Whoever isolates himself seeks his own desire; he breaks out against all sound judgment.
A fool has no delight in understanding, but only in revealing his heart.
When the wicked comes, contempt also comes, and with disgrace comes reproach.
The words of a man’s mouth are deep waters; the fountain of wisdom is a flowing brook.
It is not good to show partiality to the wicked, or to deprive the righteous of justice.
A fool’s lips enter into contention, and his mouth calls for blows.
A fool’s mouth is his ruin, and his lips are a snare to his soul.
The words of a whisperer are like delicious morsels; they go down into the inner parts.
Whoever is slack in his work is a brother to him who destroys.
The name of YHWH is a strong tower; the righteous runs into it and is safe.
A rich man’s wealth is his strong city, and like a high wall in his imagination.
Before destruction a man’s heart is haughty, but humility comes before honor.
If one gives an answer before he hears, it is his folly and shame.
A man’s spirit will endure sickness, but a crushed spirit who can bear?
The heart of the discerning acquires knowledge, and the ear of the wise seeks knowledge.
A man’s gift makes room for him and brings him before great men.
The first to state his case seems right, until his neighbor comes and examines him.
The lot puts an end to quarrels and decides between powerful contenders.
A brother offended is more unyielding than a strong city, and quarrels are like the bars of a castle.
From the fruit of a man’s mouth his stomach is satisfied; he is satisfied by the yield of his lips.
Death and life are in the power of the tongue, and those who love it will eat its fruits.
He who finds a wife finds a good thing and obtains favor from YHWH.
The poor uses entreaties, but the rich answers roughly.
A man of many companions may come to ruin, but there is a friend who sticks closer than a brother.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 19
טוֹב רָשׁ הוֹלֵךְ בְּתֻמּוֹ מֵעִקֵּשׁ שְׂפָתָיו וְהוּא כְסִיל׃
גַּם בְּלֹא־דַעַת נֶפֶשׁ לֹא־טוֹב וְאָץ בְּרַגְלַיִם חוֹטֵא׃
אִוֶּלֶת אָדָם תְּסַלֵּף דַּרְכּוֹ וְעַל־יְהוָה יִזְעַף לִבּוֹ׃
הוֹן יֹסִיף רֵעִים רַבִּים וְדָל מֵרֵעֵהוּ יִפָּרֵד׃
עֵד שְׁקָרִים לֹא יִנָּקֶה וְיָפִיחַ כְּזָבִים לֹא יִמָּלֵט׃
רַבִּים יְחַלּוּ פְנֵי נָדִיב וְכָל־הָרֵעַ לְאִישׁ מַתָּן׃
כָּל־אֲחֵי רָשׁ שְׂנֵאֻהוּ אַף כִּי מְרֵעֵהוּ רָחֲקוּ מִמֶּנּוּ רֹדֵף אֲמָרִים לֹא הֵמָּה׃
קוֹנֶה לֵב אֹהֵב נַפְשׁוֹ שֹׁמֵר תְּבוּנָה לִמְצֹא טוֹב׃
עֵד שְׁקָרִים לֹא יִנָּקֶה וְיָפִיחַ כְּזָבִים יֹאבֵד׃
לֹא־נָאוֶה לִכְסִיל תַּעֲנוּג אַף כִּי לְעֶבֶד מְשֹׁל בְּשָׂרִים׃
שֵׂכֶל אָדָם הֶאֱרִיךְ אַפּוֹ וְתִפְאַרְתּוֹ עֲבוֹר עַל־פָּשַׁע׃
נַהַם כַּכְּפִיר זַעַף מֶלֶךְ וּכְטַל עַל־עֵשֶׂב רְצוֹנוֹ׃
הַוַּת אָב לִבְנוֹ וְאִשָּׁה מְדֹנִים נִשְׁטָף דֶּלֶף מִגָּג׃
בַּיִת וָהוֹן נַחֲלַת אָבוֹת וּמֵיְהוָה אִשָּׁה מַשְׂכָּלֶת׃
עַצְלָה תַּפִּיל תַּרְדֵּמָה וְנֶפֶשׁ רְמִיָּה תִרְעָב׃
שֹׁמֵר מִצְוָה שֹׁמֵר נַפְשׁוֹ בּוֹזֵה דְרָכָיו יָמוּת׃
מַלְוֵה יְהוָה חוֹנֵן דָּל וּגְמֻלוֹ יְשַׁלֶּם־לוֹ׃
יַסֵּר בִּנְךָ כִּי יֵשׁ תִּקְוָה וְאֶל־הֲמִיתוֹ אַל־תִּשָּׂא נַפְשֶׁךָ׃
חֹמֵל עַל־עֲנִיָּה חוֹנֵן לַיהוָה וּמַלְוֵהוּ יְשַׁלֶּם־לוֹ׃
שְׁמַע עֵצָה וְקַבֵּל מוּסָר לְמַעַן תֶּחְכַּם בְּאַחֲרִיתֶךָ׃
רַבּוֹת מַחֲשָׁבוֹת בְּלֶב־אִישׁ וַעֲצַת יְהוָה הִיא תָקוּם׃
תַּאֲוָה אָדָם חַסְדּוֹ וְטוֹב רָשׁ מִכָּזָב אִישׁ׃
יִרְאַת יְהוָה לְחַיִּים וְשָׂבֵעַ יָלִין בְּלִי־יִפָּקֶד רָע׃
עַצֵּל טָמַן יָדוֹ בַּצַּלָּחַת גַּם אֶל־פִּיהוּ לֹא־יְשִׁיבֶנָּה׃
לֵץ תַּכֶּה פֶּתִי וּפֶתִי יַעְרִם דָּעַת׃
שְׁמַע מוּסָר וֶחֱדַל מֵאוֹרְחוֹת תָּעָה לְהַשְׂכִּיל דְּבָרִים׃
מְלַוֵּה יְהוָה חוֹנֵן דָּל וּגְמֻלוֹ יְשַׁלֶּם־לוֹ׃
Better is a poor man who walks in his integrity than one who is crooked in speech and is a fool.
Desire without knowledge is not good, and whoever moves too quickly misses the way.
A man’s own folly ruins his way, yet his heart rages against YHWH.
Wealth brings many friends, but a poor man is separated from his friend.
A false witness will not go unpunished, and he who breathes lies will not escape.
Many seek the favor of a generous man, and everyone is a friend to a man who gives gifts.
All a poor man’s brothers hate him; how much more do his friends go far from him! He pursues them with words, but they are gone.
Whoever gets sense loves his own soul; he who keeps understanding will discover good.
A false witness will not go unpunished, and he who breathes lies will perish.
Delight is not fitting for a fool, much less for a slave to rule over princes.
Good sense makes one slow to anger, and it is his glory to overlook an offense.
The king’s wrath is like the roaring of a lion, but his favor is like dew on the grass.
A foolish son is ruin to his father, and a quarrelsome wife is like a continual dripping.
House and wealth are inherited from fathers, but a prudent wife is from YHWH.
Slothfulness casts into a deep sleep, and an idle soul will suffer hunger.
Whoever keeps the commandment keeps his life; he who despises his ways will die.
Whoever is kind to the poor lends to YHWH, and he will repay him for his deed.
Discipline your son, for there is hope; do not set your heart on putting him to death.
Whoever is generous to the poor lends to YHWH, and he will repay him.
Listen to advice and accept instruction, that you may gain wisdom in the future.
Many are the plans in the mind of a man, but it is the purpose of YHWH that will stand.
What is desired in a man is steadfast love, and a poor man is better than a liar.
The fear of YHWH leads to life, and whoever has it rests satisfied; he will not be visited by harm.
The sluggard buries his hand in the dish and will not even bring it back to his mouth.
Strike a scoffer, and the simple will learn prudence; reprove a man of understanding, and he will gain knowledge.
Listen to advice and accept instruction, to gain wisdom for the future.
Whoever is kind to the poor lends to YHWH, and he will repay him.

>>>>>>> Proverbs 20
לֵץ הַיַּיִן הֹמֶה שֵׁכָר וְכָל־שֹׁגֶה בּוֹ לֹא יֶחְכָּם׃
נַהַם כַּכְּפִיר אֵימַת מֶלֶךְ מִתְעַבְּרוֹ חוֹטֵא נַפְשׁוֹ׃
כָּבוֹד לָאִישׁ שֶׁבֶת מֵרִיב וְכָל־אֱוִיל יִתְגַּלָּע׃
מֵחֹרֶף עָצֵל לֹא־יַחֲרֹשׁ וְשָׁאַל בַּקָּצִיר וָאָיִן׃
מַיִם עֲמֻקִּים עֵצָה בְלֶב־אִישׁ וְאִישׁ תְּבוּנָה יִדְלֶנָּה׃
רָב־אָדָם יִקְרָא אִישׁ חַסְדּוֹ וְאִישׁ אֱמוּנִים מִי יִמְצָא׃
מְהַלֵּךְ בְּתֻמּוֹ צַדִּיק אַשְׁרֵי בָנָיו אַחֲרָיו׃
מֶלֶךְ יוֹשֵׁב עַל־כִּסֵּא דִין מְזָרֶה בְּעֵינָיו כָּל־רָע׃
מִי־יֹאמַר זִכִּיתִי לִבִּי טָהַרְתִּי מֵחַטָּאתִי׃
אֶבֶן וָאֶבֶן אֵיפָה וְאֵיפָה תּוֹעֲבַת יְהוָה גַּם־שְׁנֵיהֶם׃
גַּם־בַּמַּעֲלָלָיו יִתְנַכֶּר נַעַר אִם־זַךְ וְאִם־יָשָׁר פָּעֳלוֹ׃
אֹזֶן שֹׁמַעַת וְעַיִן רֹאָה יְהוָה עָשָׂה גַּם־שְׁנֵיהֶם׃
אַל־תֶּאֱהַב שֵׁנָה פֶּן־תִּוָּרֵשׁ פְּקַח עֵינֶיךָ שְׂבַע לָחֶם׃
רַע רַע יֹאמַר הַקּוֹנֶה וְאֹזֵל לוֹ יִתְהַלָּל׃
יֵשׁ זָהָב וְרָב־פְּנִינִים וּכְלִי יְקָר שִׂפְתֵי־דָעַת׃
לָקַח בִּגְדִים כִּי עָרַב זָר וּבְעַד נָכְרִיָּה חַבְלֵהוּ׃
לֶחֶם שָׁקֶר יָעָרַב לָאִישׁ וְאַחַר יִמָּלֵא פִיהוּ חָצָץ׃
מַחֲשָׁבוֹת בְּעֵצָה תִכּוֹן וּבְתַחְבֻּלוֹת עֲשֵׂה מִלְחָמָה׃
מְגַלֶּה סוֹד הוֹלֵךְ רָכִיל וּלְפֹתֶה שְׂפָתָיו אַל־תִּתְעָרָב׃
מְקוֹר חַיִּים שֵׂכֶל בְּעָלָיו וּמוּסַר אֱוִילִים אִוֶּלֶת׃
זָרוּת לַיְהוָה אֶבֶן וָאֶבֶן וּמֹאזְנֵי מִרְמָה לֹא־טוֹב׃
מֵיְהוָה מִצְעֲדֵי גָבֶר וְאָדָם מַה־יָּבִין דַּרְכּוֹ׃
מוֹקֵשׁ אָדָם יָלַע קֹדֶשׁ וְאַחַר נְדָרִים לְבַקֵּר׃
מְלָךְ חָכָם זָרֶה רָשָׁע וְיָשֵׁר עַל־כִּסְאוֹ׃
נֵר יְהוָה נִשְׁמַת אָדָם חֹפֵשׂ כָּל־חַדְרֵי־בָטֶן׃
חֶסֶד וֶאֱמֶת יִצְּרוּ מֶלֶךְ וְסָעַד בַּחֶסֶד כִּסְאוֹ׃
תִּפְאֶרֶת בַּחוּרִים כֹּחָם וַהֲדַר זְקֵנִים שֵׂיבָה׃
חַבּוּרוֹת פֶּצַע תַּמְרִיק בְּרָע וּמַכּוֹת חַדְרֵי־בָטֶן׃
Wine is a mocker, strong drink is raging, and whoever is led astray by it is not wise.
The terror of a king is like the roaring of a lion; whoever provokes him sins against his own life.
It is an honor for a man to keep aloof from strife, but every fool will quarrel.
The sluggard does not plow in autumn; therefore he begs at harvest and has nothing.
Deep waters are the counsel in a man’s heart, but a man of understanding draws it out.
Many proclaim their own steadfast love, but a faithful man who can find?
The righteous who walks in his integrity—blessed are his children after him.
A king who sits on the throne of judgment winnows all evil with his eyes.
Who can say, “I have made my heart clean; I am pure from my sin”?
Differing weights and differing measures are both an abomination to YHWH.
Even a child makes himself known by his acts, whether his conduct is pure and upright.
The hearing ear and the seeing eye—YHWH has made them both.
Do not love sleep, lest you come to poverty; open your eyes, and you will have plenty of bread.
“It is bad, it is bad,” says the buyer, but when he goes away, then he boasts.
There is gold and abundance of jewels, but the lips of knowledge are a precious vessel.
Take a man’s garment when he has put up security for a stranger, and hold it as pledge for a foreign woman.
Bread gained by deceit is sweet to a man, but afterward his mouth will be full of gravel.
Plans are established by counsel, and by wise guidance wage war.
Whoever goes about slandering reveals secrets; therefore do not associate with a simple babbler.
The purpose in a man’s heart is like deep water, but a man of understanding draws it out.
Many a man proclaims his own loyalty, but a faithful man who can find?
